Remember we looked at SURAH AlMURSALAAT a few sessions ago. We studied the first 7 verses in which Allah was using winds to respond to the arguments of the disbelievers? What rhyme scheme did he use in that SURAH?

وَٱلْمُرْسَلَتِ عُرْفًۭا

فَٱلْعَصِفَتِ عَصْفًۭا

وَٱلنَّشِرَتِ نَشْرًۭا

فَٱلْفَرِقَتِ فَرْقًۭا

فَٱلْمُلْقِيَتِ ذِكْرًا

عُذْرًا أَوْ نُذْرًا

These 6 verses addressing 3 specific arguments? Using the example of winds for death and destruction, life and prosperity and resurrection and accountability. After this examples, he comes to his actual point - to say what he actually wanted to say, that all of this one day will become an event. Remember? To do that he changes the rhyme scheme.

إِنَّمَا تُوعَدُونَ لَوَقِعٌۭ

Because the subject has changed. The previous were examples, so he used one rhyme scheme. Now he's stating his actual intention, and so he uses another rhyme scheme. And right after that he starts another subject using a different rhyme scheme. He begins talking about the signs of the day of judgment, so he changes the rhyme scheme

فَإِذَا ٱلنُّجُومُ طُمِسَتْ ‎

وَإِذَا ٱلسَّمَآءُ فُرِجَتْ ‎

وَإِذَا ٱلْجِبَالُ نُسِفَتْ

وَإِذَا ٱلرُّسُلُ أُقِّتَتْ

لِأَىِّ يَوْمٍ أُجِّلَتْ

Once he's done mentioning the signs, he asks the disbelievers a question. And to do that he again changes the rhyme scheme. He captures the attention of the disbelievers

لِيَوْمِ ٱلْفَصْلِ ‎

وَمَآ أَدْرَىٰكَ مَا يَوْمُ ٱلْفَصْلِ

Once he's asked the question; once he's captured their attention. He begins answering the question himself, and switches the rhyme scheme once more

وَيْلٌۭ يَوْمَئِذٍۢ لِّلْمُكَذِّبِينَ

أَلَمْ نُهْلِكِ ٱلْأَوَّلِينَ

ثُمَّ نُتْبِعُهُمُ ٱلْآخِرِينَ ‎

كَذَلِكَ نَفْعَلُ بِٱلْمُجْرِمِينَ

---

<!-- section 10 (id=5793, raw_sort=10): Miracle of the book -->
Today we're going to look at a couple more AYATS from the Quran that show the miraculous perfection of this unscripted extempore speech. 

This first AYAH that I want to share with you is from SURAH EHZAAB. This is yet another example of how precise and perfect the Quran is; even when it speaks about things you and would not give a second thought to in our conversations. For example in this SURAH, Allah talks about marital issues. He begins by talking about men, and then he moves on to talk about women. So when he's speaking about men, he says:

[image 015: AI vision pending — see ../images/015.png]

Allah did not put 2 hearts inside any man. He says that and moves on to talk about women; and says:

⟪ar-quote:وَمَا جَعَلَ أَزْوَجَكُم ألتِّی تُظَهِرُونَ مِنْهُنَّ أُمَّهَتِكُمْ⟫

Let's first first go over the meaning of this AYAH. The word ⟪ar:الِرَجُلٍۢ⟫means "Man". ⟪ar:رَجُلٍۢ⟫is gender specific. The word ⟪ar:قَلْبَيْنِ⟫means "2 hearts". Its the plural form of the word "⟪ar:قَلْب⟫" which means a single heart. So ⟪ar:قَلْب⟫is singular, and ⟪ar:قَلْبَيْنِ⟫is a double plural which means 2 hearts. In Arabic you don't just have singular and plurals; you also have something called double plurals. So for any noun, you have a singular form, a double plural (meaning exactly 2) and then the general plural for more than 2.

The word in ⟪ar:جَوْفِ⟫in arabic means a hollow space. That's why a cave in Arabic is called ⟪ar:جَوْفِ⟫. Now ofcourse this verse is not literal, its metaphorical. When Allah says, we did not put 2 hearts inside a man, what he means is that faith and disbelief cannot coexist in any man. A man will believe or disbelive; he will love or he will hate; he cannot do both at the same time. But what's really interesting about this verse, is that even in its literal form, Allah did not say that he did not put 2 hearts inside any human being.

Don't men and women both have a single heart?  So then why did Allah single out men in this ayah? Cause he specifically says ⟪ar:لِرَجُلٍۢ⟫which means man. Allah could have simply said...

⟪ar-quote:مَّا جَعَلَ ٱللَّهُ لی النَّاسِ مِّن قَلْبَيْنِ فِى جَوْفِهِ⟫

Allah did not put 2 hearts inside any human being. That would have covered both. But Allah excluded women from it. And this is perfection in it's literal form; not LITERARY form, but LITERAL form. Because  you see, a woman can get pregnant! And when a woman gets pregnant, how many hearts are inside? It could be two or more. So Allah says he did not put 2 hearts inside any man! SubhanAllah! Even in it's literal form Quran is so incredibly perfect! Nobody can play devils advocate and say, "Well what about women? They can get pregnant!". No you can't! Allah just referred to man in the verse ⟪ar:لِرَجُلٍۢ⟫! SubhanAllah!

See, it is impossible for us as human beings, to be so hypersensitive to the content as we're speaking. And this Quran is coming as an unscripted speech, passsages upon passages at a time, and yet it is so sensitive to the most minute level of detail. Show me this kind of perfection in any other spoken conversation, anywhere in the world.

---

This next miracle that I want to show you today, is also related to the profound nature of the imagery of the Quran. As we've seen previously, Quran is a very coherent; very connected text. One part of a verse describes the other. Words that are going to be said in the future, have an influence on words that are coming in the beginning. So now this is a verse from SURAH SABA. Allah says....

**https://quran.com/34/2

> ⟪ar:يَعْلَمُ مَا يَلِجُ فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ وَمَا يَخْرُجُ مِنْهَا وَمَا يَنزِلُ مِنَ ٱلسَّمَاءِ وَمَا يَعْرُجُ فِيهَا ۚ وَهُوَ ٱلرَّحِيمُ ٱلْغَفُورُ⟫
> *He knows what enters into the earth and what comes out of it, and what comes down from the sky and what rises to it, and He is the constantly merciful, exceedingly forgiving.*
> — **Quran 34:2** *(from image; see _provenance.json for validation)*
  (image preserved at ../images/016.png)
  *Note:* Quran 34:2 (Sura Saba'). Used to illustrate the symmetric/chiastic ordering inside a single verse — earth/sky and entry/exit pairings.
**Lets go over the translation fist
⟪ar-quote:يَعْلَمُ مَا يَلِجُ فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ⟫

He knows what enters into the earth
⟪ar-quote:وَمَا يَخْرُجُ مِنْهَا⟫

and what comes out of it,
⟪ar-quote:وَمَا يَنزِلُ مِنَ ٱلسَّمَآءِ⟫

and what comes down from the sky,
⟪ar-quote:وَمَا يَعْرُجُ فِيهَاۚ⟫

and what rises to it....
⟪ar-quote:وَهُوَ ٱلرَّحِيمُ ٱلْغَفُورُ⟫

And he is the constantly merciful and exceedingly forgiving.

Now this is a very interesting ayah. If you notice the part in green, what do you see, the ayah ending in? ⟪ar:وَهُوَ ٱلرَّحِيمُ ٱلْغَفُورُ⟫ . Now if you recite the Quran often enough, you may have noticed that you don't normally see the words ⟪ar:ٱلرَّحِيمُ ٱلْغَفُورُ⟫come together. Instead you always see the words ⟪ar:ٱلْغَفُورُ ٱلرَّحِيمُ⟫ used together. That's the general theme in the Quran. Over 70 times he uses the words⟪ar:ٱلْغَفُورُ ٱلرَّحِيم⟫ُ in the Quran.

⟪ar-quote:قالَ سَوْفَ أَسْتَغْفِرُ لَكُمْ رَبِّىٓ ۖ إِنَّهُۥ هُوَ ٱلْغَفُورُ ٱلرَّحِيمُ⟫

⟪ar-quote:قَالَ رَبِّ إِنِّى ظَلَمْتُ نَفْسِى فَٱغْفِرْ لِى فَغَفَرَ لَهُۥٓ ۚ إِنَّهُۥ هُوَ ٱلْغَفُورُ ٱلرَّحِيمُ⟫

⟪ar-quote:ثُمَّ أَفِيضُوا۟ مِنْ حَيْثُ أَفَاضَ ٱلنَّاسُ وَٱسْتَغْفِرُوا۟ ٱللَّهَ ۚ إِنَّ ٱللَّهَ غَفُورٌۭ رَّحِيمٌۭ⟫

⟪ar-quote:قُلْ إِن كُنتُمْ تُحِبُّونَ ٱللَّهَ فَٱتَّبِعُونِى يُحْبِبْكُمُ ٱللَّهُ وَيَغْفِرْ لَكُمْ ذُنُوبَكُمْ ۗ وَٱللَّهُ غَفُورٌۭ رَّحِيمٌۭ⟫

So everywhere else in the Quran, Allah says ⟪ar:غَفُورٌۭ رَّحِيمٌۭ⟫ . Which again, means forgiving comma merciful. But this is the ONLY place in the entire Quran where Allah says, ⟪ar:ٱلرَّحِيمُ ٱلْغَفُورُ⟫. merciful comma forgiving. So what up with that? Now we know that every word has to be in its proper place. So if the Allah has changed the sequence here, there has to be some profound wisdom behind it.

Before I share that with you, there is something I need you to understand about forgiveness. Everytime Allah uses the words ⟪ar:غَفُورٌۭ رَّحِيمٌۭ⟫ at the end of an AYAH, you will find the beginning of that verse talking about human beings in one way or other. That's important to note! Because when it comes to human beings, we need to be forgiven first, and then we become deserving of Allah's mercy. That's the proper sequence as far as we are concerned.

And if you think about it, this sequence applies to us, in our relationships with one another as well. There is a saying in Arabic

⟪ar-quote:انَّ الدَّرءَ المَفْسَدَۃ مُقَدَّم عَلیٰ جَلبِ المَسْلَحَۃ⟫

If you have a dirty glass, and you want to drink juice, what do you have to do first? Clean the glass. So clean out the negative element, before you can add the positive element. Forgiveness cleans out the negative emotion from the heart; and mercy, is obviously then the positive element that follows. So lets say, if your friend has offended you, and you are angry with her, you will need to forgive her first, before you can sincerely begin showing her any more favors again. Right? So it's the same principle. In order to gain Allah's mercy, we first need to gain His forgiveness. Forgiveness is an attribute that affects only human beings. If there is no mention of human beings, there is no need for forgiveness. Have you every forgiven your car? When your toaster burns your toast, do you ever have to forgive it? to feel the same way about making toasts? When you hit your foot at the corner of a door, do you go back to it later and say, "I forgive you door!". I hope not! Because forgiveness is associated only with human beings. You will forgive your friend, your brother, your sister. So the presence of this word ⟪ar:غَفُورٌۭ⟫indicates, that this verse is in fact talking about human beings. It's just not literal, it's implied.

Another interesting fact, is that wherever in the Quran, Allah talks about knowledge, you will find the mention of the word "mercy" in that passage. Knowledge is directly affiliated with mercy everywhere in the Quran. Because for us to have the knowledge of Allah, is the greatest mercy of all! And the greatest proof of that concept from the Quran is the amazing verse:

⟪ar-quote:الرحمن علم القرآن⟫

The intensely merciful "taught" the Quran; which is knowledge and education.

Now let's read this verse again:

⟪ar-quote:يَعْلَمُ مَا يَلِجُ فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ⟫..⟪ar-quote:وَمَا يَخْرُجُ مِنْهَا..⟫⟪ar-quote:وَمَا يَنزِلُ مِنَ ٱلسَّمَآءِ⟫⟪ar-quote:وَمَا يَعْرُجُ فِيهَاۚ⟫.. ⟪ar-quote:وَهُوَ ٱلرَّحِيمُ ٱلْغَفُورُ⟫

He knows what enters into the earth and what comes out of it; and what comes down from the sky, and what rises to it. And he is the constantly merciful and exceedingly forgiving.

When a farmer hears these words, that Allah know what enters into the earth, what does he think of? Seeds!  and when he hears the words, Allah knows what comes out, he thinks of what? A plant! But if we take a deeper look, we human beings will also enter the earth one day! And we too will come out of the earth one day! On the day of judgment. Allah says, He has complete knowledge of what enters into the earth, and what comes out of it. Now this could refer to the seeds and plants; but it also, most certainly holds true for us human beings. Because we too will enter the earth one day and come out of it. If you look at the next part of the ayah he says...

⟪ar-quote:وَمَا يَنزِلُ مِنَ ٱلسَّمَآءِ وَمَا يَعْرُجُ فِيهَا⟫

He knows what's coming down from the sky and what rises up to it. From the farmers perspetive what is that? Rain! But from the perspective of human beings, what's coming down from the sky? Revelation! The word of Allah coming down from the sky. Rain is a mercy from Allah; and this revelation is a mercy from Allah. 

Now once the revelation comes down, and people hear it, they either act according to it, or they don't act according to it. So what's going back up to the sky? Their deeds! Their deeds! Their actions are going back up for evaluation. You understand? Let's read this verse again with this understanding:

⟪ar-quote:⟪ar-quote:يَعْلَمُ مَا⟫يَلِجُ فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ وَمَا يَخْرُجُ مِنْهَا⟫

Human beings enter the earth when they die; human beings come out of the earth on the day of judgment.

At the time of death, what do people need most? Mercy or forgiveness? Mercy! Because death is a very difficult transition. So Allah brings the word mercy first.

But when people are raised from the ground on the day of judgment, what are they going to need most of all? Mercy or forgiveness? They're going to need Allah's forgiveness. On the day of judgment, the thing we all will need most, is Allah's forgiveness. So Allah ends the verse with forgiveness. SubhanAllah!

Now let's look at the next part

⟪ar-quote:وَمَا يَنزِلُ مِنَ ٱلسَّمَآءِ وَمَا يَعْرُجُ فِيهَا⟫

Revelation is coming down from the sky; and human deeds and actions are rising back up to Allah for evaluation. What comes down from the sky again? Revelation! And revelation is Allah's mercy, yes? So Allah brings the word "mercy" first.

And what goes up to the sky again? Human actions, which need what? Forgiveness. Therefore he ends with the word forgiveness. Subhan Allah! The only place in the Quran where mercy is first, forigiveness is second. SubhanAllah!

Can you appreciate, how perfect this speech is, even at the most minute level? You be the judge and honestly tell me if human beings are capable of this kind of sensitivity to details in unscripted, impromptu conversations.  SubhanAllah! Just look at what we hold in our hands - This incredibly miraculous Quran. I really hope the next time we pickup the Quran in our hands, we all have a completely different appreciation for it.

Why and How the Quran was compiled

So everything I shared with you so far had to do with the miracle of speech. When the ancient Arabs heard this message, they were completely taken by it. They were completely defeated by its power. They were incapacitated; left incapable of a response, and they had to submit to the fact, that this just could not be human speech.

Now I want to transition into the miracle of the book. Because that is how we perceive the Quran. When you and I think of the Quran, we think of a book! The image that comes to our mind is that of a printed book, with beautiful calligraphy, and glossy pages. But when the companions thought of the Quran, the image of the prophet's face came in there minds; and his voice rang in their ears. You see? For them, they could not think of the Quran without thinking about the prophet (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). We can do that! When we think of the Quran, we do not think about the prophet! We just think of a book. But this was impossible for them to do. Because the only time they heard the Quran, it was from the mouth of the prophet (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). So to them the message and the messenger were inseparable.

Now the Quran is revealed bit by bit over a period of 23 years, and it is being memorized word for word; syllable for syllable by the companions. Do you know who was the first HAFIZ of the Quran? Who was the first person in the world to completely memorize this message by heart? It was our beloved prophet (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). He was the first HAFIZ of the Quran; the ultimate HAFIZ. Every other HAFIZ in the world, is trying to fulfill the SUNNAH of the messenger (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). And the Prophet himself was extremely meticulous about the integrity of the Quran. He constantly recited the SURAHS in public as they were arranged at the time. Jibraeel (AS) would review the entire Quran with the Prophet (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) once a year, during the month of Ramadan. But during his last year, JIBRAEEL (AS) reviewed it twice with him. And as he's reviewing the Quran, the companions are listening and brushing up.

Now just to give you a little historical background, the Quran is also being documented as it is being revealed. Rasul Allah(Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) appointed a scribe named "Zayd Ibn Sabit" to write down the verses as they were being revealed. When a verse or a passage was revealed, he would recite it in public; but then he would also have ⟪ar:زید ان ثابت⟫, not only write that verse down; he would also tell him where this block of revelation needed to be positioned in relation to previous revelations. And all of this documentation is taking place on the leather of gazelle and camels. So as revelation is coming down, the Quran is not only being documented, it is also being compiled in a very specific order, under the supervision of the messenger himself (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam).

But despite this documentation, the primary style of preserving the Quran is still through memorization. The companions are direclty memorizing the verses; teaching it to their families; reciting it in SALAAT; reciting it in the MASJID. And there is this constant review and revision process taking place. They're not using the written scripture as a reference. They don't need to! Because they know the entire Quran by heart! BTW, do you know how extensively the companions recited the Quran? They would recite the entire Quran, from beginning to end, once a week. What they did is, they divided the Quran into 7 sections called MANAZIL (or sections). Why 7? Because there are seven days in a week. So they could recite one MANZIL (or one section) every single day. So on the first day the companions would recite 3 SURAHS; on the second day they would recite 5 SURAHS; the third day they would recite 7 SURAHS; the next day they would recite 9 SURAHS; the fifth day they would recite 11 SURAHS; sixth day they would recite 13 SURAHS; on the final day, they would recite the remaining 65 SURAHS; because as we know, the SURAHS become shorter towards the end. This is how extensively the entire Quran was recited by the companions. This is how important this message was to them. Look how far we've come from that time.

Anyway, so there are these two kinds of preservations taking place. The primary mode of preservation is through memorization; and the secondary mode of preservation is through ⟪ar:زید ان ثابت⟫ documenting the verses under the supervision of the prophet himself. And so the records are maintained; and they're proplery indexed; and made sure that they were complete and accurate according to prophet’s instructions.

In the year 632 Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) passes away. But by that time, many of the companions had already memorized the Quran perfectly. ⟪ar:ابی ابن کعب⟫  was considered the best HAAFIZ among all of them. A year later, in 633 the battle of Yamama takes place against the people of NAJD. And the reason for that battle was that one of them had declared himself to be a prophet. In that battle, many of these HUFFAZ are martyred. That's when the need of compiling the Quran into a book form was realized. And guess who is given the responsibility to compile the Quran? The prophet's scribe - ⟪ar:زید ان ثابت⟫. And the criteria for this compilation, was that for every piece of Quran that was written in the life of the prophet, 2 witnesses need to step forth; who are HAFIZ of the Quran themselves; and confirm that yes! Indeed this is the verse that was revealed to the prophet, and this is the order in which he structured them! This is the SURAH in which this verse is supposed to go. Two witnesses for every single verse of the Quran. This is how the entire Quran was put together in the form of the book that we have today.

Ordinal accuracy

Now fast forward to 2016. Computers have long been invented; and the power of computing has sky-rocketed. Today we use computers to record every single piece of information. We have search engines optimized to deliver more and more relevant content in less and less time. And so with these enhancements in technology, people began converting the Quran into a digital form, by saving it into databases. And then they began doing all sorts of search optimizations to figure out what word occurs how many times in the Quran. They started digitally disecting the Quran - horizontally and vertically - to perform all sorts of analysis on it.

But when the Quran was being revealed, none of these technologies existed. There was no such thing as a database! There was no such thing as a search engine. So today, if you ask, "How many times is the word "Allah" used in the entire Quran?", that can be answered very easily. All you have to do is go online, and you'll find some database that spits out the answer in a second. But could you do this back then? Could you just ask one of the companions who has memorized the book, Excuse me Sir! How many times does the Quran say the word AYAH? He'd have to start from the FATEHA and keep count till he reached the end. They couldnt do that. Because they had Quran preserved in their hearts and mind. And human brains do not operate like that. If I ask you, "I have been doing these sessions for the past 10 weeks. How many times did I use the word "dammit"?. There's no way for you to answer that. And even if you did throw out out a number, would I know for sure? I wouldn't!

Now before I share with the results of the analysis done on the Quran, I want you to understand something about the Quran. Do you know what the fundamental message of Quran is? It has many many messages, but do you know what's the common thread running through the fabric of the entire Quran? It's a call to establish balance. There is an entire SURAH dedicated to this balance - SURAH REHMAN

⟪ar-quote:‏ٱلرَّحْمَنُ ؛ عَلَّمَ ٱلْقُرْآن⟪ar-quote:؛⟫خَلَقَ ٱلْإِنسَن⟪ar-quote:؛⟫عَلَّمَهُ ٱلْبَيَان⟪ar-quote:؛⟫ٱلشَّمْسُ وَٱلْقَمَرُ بِحُسْبَان⟪ar-quote:؛⟫وَٱلنَّجْمُ وَٱلشَّجَرُ يَسْجُدَان⟪ar-quote:؛⟫وَٱلسَّمَآءَ رَفَعَهَا وَوَضَعَ ٱلْمِيزَانَ⟫
He begins by talking about how he created this universe in a balanced way; and then he commands us to establish that same balance in our lives

⟪ar-quote:أَلَّا تَطْغَوْا۟ فِى ٱلْمِيزَانِ ⟪ar-quote:⟪ar-quote:؛⟫⟫ وَأَقِيمُوا۟ ٱلْوَزْنَ بِٱلْقِسْطِ وَلَا تُخْسِرُوا۟ ٱلْمِيزَانَ⟫

Do no transgress the balance. Establish balance in everything in your life and don't fall short.

So with that background information in mind, now let's look at some of the results that analysts have found, by running various word searches on the Quran. They ran a count for words to see how many times a particular word occurs in the Quran.

---

This book uses the word ⟪ar:الدنیا⟫ several times in the Quran, which means "this world". It mentions the word DUNIYA ⟪ar:دنیا⟫ times. Did anybody know that back then? They had no idea! You know what's so interesting? This book also uses the word ⟪ar:أخرۃ⟫, which means the next life - exactly 115 times. What is the message of the Quran? A call to balance! How many times does he use the word DUNIYA? 115 times. How many times does he balance it with the usage of its counter part (AKHIRA)? 115 times. Could this be a coincidence. Is it possible that maybe? somehow? accidentally these two words happen to have the exact same count in the book? Is that possible? Sure - its possible! It could be pure coincidence. Why not? OK!

This book uses the word ⟪ar:الملائکۃ⟫(angels) 88 times; and it also uses the word ⟪ar:شیاطین⟫(devils) exactly 88 times. Okay! So 2 coincidences! It can happen! Why not?

The word for LIFE ⟪ar:الحیاۃ⟫occurs 145 times in the entire Quran. You want to take a guess of what also occurs 145 times in the Quran? Death! The word death occurs in the Quran exactly 145 times.

And there are other times when the Quran says, "they say or they said".  So QUL is when Allah commands the messenger to say something. یقول or قال is when people say something to the messenger.

Do you know what the word WASAT means in Arabic? It is used when something is exactly in the middle, or the center of something. Allah says in SURAH ALBAQARAH (which mind you, is the longest SURAH of the Quran), he says:

<!-- section 11 (id=6793, raw_sort=11): Structural Miracle -->
We've began exploring the miracles of the "book" in the previous session. As I showed you, Quran is miraculous in its form of speech, as well as in its book form. And interesting Allah has used both words (message as well as book) to describe the Quran:

⟪ar-quote:وَمَا عَلَى ٱلرَّسُولِ إِلَّا ٱلْبَلَغُ ٱلْمُبِينُ⟫

And the only obligation the prophet has it to deliver this clear message. An then it also says:

⟪ar-quote:ذَلِكَ ٱلْكِتَبُ لَا رَيْبَ ۛ فِيهِ⟫

So both words ⟪ar:بلاغ⟫and ⟪ar:کتاب⟫are used for the Quran. We began the sessions by exploring the miracles of ⟪ar:بلاغ⟫(of speech), and now we're exploring the miracles of the ⟪ar:کتاب⟫.

OK, so we look at the Quran as a book. But is it? Is it really a book? Does the quran, even in its compiled book form, does it fit the structure of a book? Let's first try to determine that. Is Quran truly a book? We've all read books haven't we? So we all know something about the organization of a book, right? What does every book normally have? It has a table of contents, chapters, paragraphs, lines, maybe an index at the end, right? Now let's look at the Quran's structure.

The Quran is made up of how many SURAHS? 114 Surahs.  How is the word "SURAH" translated in English? Chapters! So in other words the Quran has 114 chapters, right? Chapter 1, Ch2, Ch3, Ch4. Now tell me, in any regular book, is Ch4 based on Ch 3? Yes it is! Now what is stated in in Chapter 3 in the book, is it again repeated in Chapter 4? and then again in Chapter 5 and then again in Chapter 6? No it's not! There is no repetition. There is some sort of logical and sequential progression across all chapters. The story line moves forward. Isn't it?

Does the Quran repeat itself across multiple chapters? Yes! It has already stated the story of Moosa (AS), in chapter 2, it does it again in 3, again in 4, again in 5. There are over 70 passages, related just to the story of Moosa (AS); and they are all over the place, in almost every single SURAH of the Quran. And these stories are not in chronological order either. They are in all sorts of random order! SURAH 1 does not begin with the birth of MOOSA (AS); and then his adoption by FIRON in SURAH 2; then him being raised in SURAH 3. No! The passages that talk about MOOSA (AS) are in no particular chronological order in the Quran. They're scattered randomly all over the place. But that's not how a chapter of any book is organized, is it? so In other words, these are not really chapters, are they?

Another thing is, that if you examine the individual chapters of the Quran, various topics are covered with sudden switches from one topic to another, and then back again. Allah begins by talking about EISA (AS), and then he suddenly switches to talking about the afterlife for a few verses, and then returns back to the story of EISA AS; which is what I showed you in the session on rhyme scheme. That is again, not how a chapter is written. In other words, what we classify as "chapters" is something else. A story book has chapters, but as we read them, the chronology moves forward; and we don't find random jumps and switches in the story line.  So you cannot compare a SURAH to a chapter. SURAH is Quran's own proprietary term. There is no such thing as a SURAH in any other book.

Now what is a SURAH made up of? AYAATS! What is the word "AYAH" translated as in English? What comes to mind when you hear the word "verse"? Poems! Songs! or in a biblical context, verses of the bible. So normally in life, when you hear the word "verse", you think of a song, or a poem or the bible. Now the Quran is very adamant in letting us know that this content is not poetry:

⟪ar-quote:وما علمنہ الشعر و ما ھو بقول شاعر⟫

We did not teach you poetry! This Quran is not poetry. The last thing we should be thinking, as Muslims, is that this is poetry. And the last thing we should be thinking, is that this content of the Quran has been plagurized from the bible. But the 2 things that come to mind when you hear the word "verse", is poem and bible. Maybe not so much to our minds, because we're so conditioned to this, but to the average non muslim, that's the first thing that comes to their mind. In other words, the word AYAH is unique. No other book has AYATS. It's a unique term!

You can't even think of an AYAH as a sentence. Because a sentence needs to have a subject and a predicate. In the Quran, can you think of one single word that is a complete AYAH? AL-REHMAN! Just one word that is a complete AYAH! Have you every read a sentence that just said "The Magnificent" "The Benevolent". No! You can have a title like that, but you can't have a sentence that just says, "the Merciful".  But in the Quran, just one single word can qualify to be a complete AYAH.

But then there are also cases where multiple AYAATS can come together to form one single sentence.

⟪ar-quote:الحمد للہ رب العالمین، الرحمن الرحیم مالک یوم الدین⟫

These are 3 seprate AYATS; but grammatically they form one sentence. AL-REHMAN was a single word, but a complete AYAH. But FATEHA begins with 3 individual AYATS, that grammatically form one single sentence. You don't have this in any other book, in any language of the world.

Then there are entire passages, entire paragraphs dedicated to explaining a subject, but they are just one single AYAH

⟪ar-quote:مُّحَمَّدٌۭ رَّسُولُ ٱللَّهِ ۚ وَٱلَّذِينَ مَعَهُۥٓ أَشِدَّآءُ عَلَى ٱلْكُفَّارِ رُحَمَآءُ بَيْنَهُمْ ۖ تَرَىٰهُمْ رُكَّعًۭا سُجَّدًۭا يَبْتَغُونَ فَضْلًۭا مِّنَ ٱللَّهِ وَرِضْوَنًۭا ۖ سِيمَاهُمْ فِى وُجُوهِهِم مِّنْ أَثَرِ ٱلسُّجُودِ ۚ ذَلِكَ مَثَلُهُمْ فِى ٱلتَّوْرَىٰةِ ۚ وَمَثَلُهُمْ فِى ٱلْإِنجِيلِ كَزَرْعٍ أَخْرَجَ شَطْـَٔهُۥ فَـَٔازَرَهُۥ فَٱسْتَغْلَظَ فَٱسْتَوَىٰ عَلَىٰ سُوقِهِۦ يُعْجِبُ ٱلزُّرَّاعَ لِيَغِيظَ بِهِمُ ٱلْكُفَّارَ ۗ وَعَدَ ٱللَّهُ ٱلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا۟ وَعَمِلُوا۟ ٱلصَّلِحَتِ مِنْهُم مَّغْفِرَةًۭ وَأَجْرًا عَظِيمًۢا⟫

An entire paragraph in SURAH AlFATHA, but one single AYAH of the Quran! So when we are looking at the verses of the Quran, we cannot confine them to any one literary form. There is only one word you can use to describe an AYAH, and that is the word AYAH itself. Both, SURAH and AYATS, are proprietary terms of the Quran. Copyrights of Allah! This makes the structure of the Quran unique, and unlike any other book in the world.

Then if you further examine the structure of the Quran, you cannot categorize the contents of the Quran in any specific order. Are the Meccan surahs first and then the Madani Surahs? No! They're all mixed in together. Is the shortest SURAH first and the longest SURAH last? Or is the longest SURAH first and the shortest SURAH last? No! So it's not going by size order. Are all the stories of the prophets mentioned first, and then the laws and then then the wisdoms? No! So it's not going by subject order either. It does not follow any kind of chronology. Every other book in the world has some kind of an order; a sequence, a progression; but not the Quran. Even the bibles, the old and the new testaments have an order; but not the Quran! And this is so evident, that it drives orientalists crazy! And that's the greatest criticsim they have about the Quran, that there is no order to the Quran! And when you don't have order, what do you have? You have chaos! So that's their conclusion about the Quran; that the quran is chaotic in its structure (⟪ar:نعوذ باللہ⟫).

The problem is, that these orientalist, they try to fit the structure of this divine message into the mold of their man-made structure of a book. And this is impossible, because the Quran has its own unique structure that is unlike any other structure of any other book in the word. And that is the miracle we are going to look at today.

---

So then what is this remarkable structure of the Quran?

The Quran's structure is actually symmetrical. It has a circular composition, which is also called a "Ring Composition". What that means is, that there is a very clear correspondence, a very clear corelation, a distinct connection, between the beginning of a surah and the end of the surah.

[diagram: Same chiastic-pairing diagram as in binder 34 ch153 img 002 — coloured dots A B C D paired by green arrows inside a red circle, illustrating ring composition.]
  (see ../images/017.png)
  *Note:* Reused chiasm diagram. Same pedagogical content as elsewhere; this is a content-duplicate but a byte-different image.

So imagine you cut out a perfect circle from a sheet of paper, and then you fold it in half on its center, you'll see that every single point on the right side will meet the exact same point on the left side. To make this simple and easy to understand, in the English language, or any language for that matter; there is a structure called a palindrome. A palindrome is a word that reads the same way forwards and backwards. Like: BOB, MADAM,  RACECAR.

[diagram: Single chiastic-row 'R A C E C A R' around a central dark-blue 'E'; purple/red arrows on each end show inward symmetry — the palindrome analogy for ring composition.]
  (see ../images/018.png)
  *Note:* RACECAR palindrome diagram (bottom row from the prior two-row version).

A palandrome has a symmetrical or ciruclar structure; and so does the Quran. The entire Quran is structured as a palandrome. In other words, if you take a surah, and split it in half, you'll see that the first half, perfectly mirror the second half. This is how the entire Quran is structured. It is called "Ring Composition"

Ka'ba is the new qibla (142 - 152). F. Details of how Muslims will be tested (153 - 177). G. Deliverance of Shariah to Muslims (178 - 253). H. Allah's creation and knowledge (254 - 284). I. Faith vs. Disbelief (285 - 286).*

Why Circular?

So let's discuss why Allah chose this circular structure. A circle is a very special geometric shape in our religion., especially in the creation of this universe. We all know that a circle exists because of its center. If there is no center, there is no circle. All of Allah's creation is based on this one shape. You see how everything in nature is circular. The earth is circular; it's rotation is circular; all processes and sub-processes within nature are cyclic. Seasons repeat in a cycle; planets are circular; the orbits in which they rotate is circular; and as they revolve, they also rotate on their axis, which is also a circular motion; day and night repeat in a cycle. The practices of ISLAM are cyclic (SALAAT, ZAKAAT, SAUM) they all repeat every year; TAWAAF around the kaaba is circular. right?

So why ciricle? Because circle has continuity. A circle is an endless loop. The word Quran literally means something that is read over and over again. Beacuse the Quran doesn't stop after reciting it once. Once we've completed its recitation, we starts all over again. It's recitation is constant! It is continuous and it is endless. And a circle cannot exist without a center? The circle exists to prove the existence of its center, right? The circle exists because the center exits! So whose existence is the circular structure of the Quran proving? Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala)! Quran's circular structure is the ultimate proof of the existence of Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala)! He is at the heart; at the center of all creation!

  (see ../images/021.png)

The surah begins with Hazrat Yusuf AS having a dream that 11 stars and the sun and moon are prostrating to him; The surah ends with his dream being actualized

Second topic: His brothers plot against him. Second last topic: his brothers realize their mistake and learn their lesson

Third topic: The ministers wife tries to seduce him. Third last topic: The ministers wife confesses her act

Fourth topic: Elite women of the city try to seduce him. Fourth to last topic: They confess their crime

Fifth topic: Yousuf AS goes to prison. Fifth topic from the end: Yousuf AS is freed from prison

Sixth topic: The king has a dream. Sixth topic from the end: The kings dream is interpretted

SubhanAllah!

You know what it means? ⟪ar:وَلَمْ يَكُن لَّهُۥ كُفُوًا أَحَدٌۢ⟫ - That there is no one comparable to him. SubhanAllah! The first AYAH perfectly aligns with the last AYAH

The next verse says, ⟪ar:ٱللَّهُ ٱلصَّمَدُ⟫, The word SAMAD means "absolute". Someone that does not require anyone or anything else to survive. Someone who is completely self-sufficient is called SAMAD. Now look what this verse connects to:  ⟪ar:لَمْ يَلِدْ وَلَمْ يُولَدْ⟫. He is not a son, nor does he have a son. He begets not, nor was he begotten. Why? Because he his SAMAD. Again, perfect symmetry. SubhanAllah!

  *Note:* Sura al-Kafirun chiastic structure (1↔6, 2↔5, 3↔4).

In this image, I've aligned the AYATS in the circular pattern for you. So I have the first and the last AYAH together on the first line; then the second and the second last; and finally the third and the third last AYATS. The theme of this SURAH is a conversation with the disbelievers. It is about a separation and a clear disconnect of the messenger (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) from the disbelievers of Mecca. Allah is abandoning the disbelievers in this SURAH, and the messanger is being commanded to tell them, that from this day forth the believers path, is completely separate from the disbelievers path.

The first AYAH begins with a command: ⟪ar:قُلْ يَٓأَيُّهَا ٱلْكَفِرُونَ⟫, "Say to the disbelievers!". Say what? ⟪ar:لَكُمْ دِينُكُمْ وَلِىَ دِينِ⟫ . To you belongs your religion, and to us belong ours religion. The entire essence of the SURAH, perfectly captured in the first and last verse of the SURAH - SubhanAllah!

The second verse is: ⟪ar:لَآ أَعْبُدُ مَا تَعْبُدُونَ⟫, I do not worship the one you worship. Look at verse it connects to: ⟪ar:وَلَآ أَنتُمْ عَبِدُونَ مَآ أَعْبُدُ⟫ , nor will you worship the one I worship. In the previous set, we saw Allah declaring his disengagment from the disbelievers by saying, you have your way, and we have ours. This second combination explains the reason why! Because I (meaning the messanger); I do not worship the idols you worship! And you will not worship the Allah I worship! Both AYATS perfectly aligned in meaning.

The third set is: ⟪ar:وَلَآ أَنتُمْ عَبِدُونَ مَآ أَعْبُدُ⟫ , And you will not worship the one I worship, and ⟪ar:وَلَآ أَنَا۠ عَابِدٌۭ مَّا عَبَدتُّمْ⟫; and I do not worship the idols you woship. Its the same message in a mirrored form. The previous set begins with the messenger and the reason for disconnecting from the disbelivers; this set begins with the reason for disconnecting from the the disbelievers (Because you guys do not worship the one I worship) and connects with the affirmation of the believers (and I will not worship those that you worship).  SubhanAllah! Again we find prefect symmetry in its structure.

---

Let's look at another one. SURAH AlKAUSAR. This context of this SURAH is that it was revealed when the 4th and last child of the messenger (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) passed away. When ABU JAHAL heard the news, he came out of his house celebrating. He took a stick and started banging it on a piece of metal, saying بتر محمد! بتر محمد! . The lineage of Muhammad (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) has ended! And this dispicable, disgusting man لعنۃ اللہ علیہ is the uncle of the messenger! He is celebrating the death of his nephews son. And this deeply hurts the messenger (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). And as soon as he feels the pain of those words, Allah reveals this SURAH, to console his beloved messenger.

I love this one!

> ⟪ar:إِنَّا أَعْطَيْنَاكَ الْكَوْثَرَ ﴿١﴾ فَصَلِّ لِرَبِّكَ وَانْحَرْ ﴿٢﴾ إِنَّ شَانِئَكَ هُوَ الْأَبْتَرُ ﴿٣﴾⟫
> — **Quran 108:None** *(from image; see _provenance.json for validation)*
  (image preserved at ../images/024.png)
  *Note:* Sura al-Kawthar chiastic structure with verse 2 as pivot.

Allah says, ⟪ar:إِنَّآ أَعْطَيْنَكَ ٱلْكَوْثَرَ⟫, Indeed we have granted you abundance. Who has been granted abundance? the messenger (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). Now if you connect this to the last verse, in which Allah is speaking to the disbelievers - those who make the messenger sad and angry, Allah says ⟪ar:إِنَّ شَانِئَكَ هُوَ ٱلْأَبْتَرُ⟫. Indeed the one who hurts you, makes you angry, will be the ones whose lineage will be completely cut off. So in the first set, we find extreme aboundance mentioned; and the last set talks about complete deprevation.

But now look at the middle AYAH. ⟪ar:فصل لربک وانحر⟫. This AYAH has two parts. The first part is ⟪ar:فَصَلِّ لِرَبِّكَ⟫. So pray to your master; ⟪ar:وَٱنْحَرْ⟫and sacrifice. What does prayer create? Abundance! And what does sacrifice create? Shortage! When we sacrifice animals at the time of HAJJ, does that create abundance in the stock or shortage? It creates shortage. When we desire abundance from Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) what do we do? SALAAT. SubhanAllah! The first AYAH talks about infinite abundance, the last one talks about complete deprevation and shortage. The first part of the middle AYAH talks about the abundance; and the second part of the middle AYAH talks about shortage. They perfectly align with each other. SubhanAllah! You can't make this stuff up!

Now you tell me who can speak extemporaneously and compile like that? 23 years of an impromptu speech, that is not only perfect in its choice of words; that is not only perfect in its order and sequence of words; that is not only perfect in its conciseness; that is not only perfectly balanced in its count of words; but is also perfectly circular and symmetrical in its AYATS.

When people did their research on the structure of the Quran, this is what they found. That it is incredible symmetrical. The companions didn't know about this! And just to be very clear, there is no call to action in relaizing the symmetrical structure of the Quran. It's not like from this day forth, you start reading the Quran in this circular way. Absolutely not! We will continue reciting the Quran the way we normally do today. Just as there's not call to action by knowing how many times a word is repeated in the Quran. But it's certainly marvellous and facinating evidence of the divinity of this book. That there is no way, human beings can speak symmetrically. There is no way we can have a conversation, and compose a ring as we're speaking. It is ABSOLUTELY impossible. The purpose of experiencing these miracles, is to remove doubts, and add conviction to the divinity of this book.

I challenge anyone in the group to tell me about their day in this symmetrical way! You can't even tell me what you had for breakfast symmetrically. Because we human beings cannot think and speak like that.

So now, hoping that you all are completely mesmerized by this structure of the Quran, let me tell you, that it gets even better! When people started analyzing the Quran, they found out that it is not only symmetrical and circular in the topics of its SURAH; it is also symmetrical within the various passages and AYATS. It's not just symmetircal at the "macro" level, it is also symmetrical at the "micro" level. Not only are the SURAHS coming together in a ring composition, various AYAATS and passages within the SURAHS are also exhibiting a ring composition. And then not just the AYATS are in a ring composition, individual sentences within the AYAATS are also in a ring composition. In some cases, two completely disconnected surahs come together to form a ring composition; and in other cases two consequitive ayats come together to form a ring. Allahu Akbar!

⟪ar-quote:فبای آلاء ربکما تکذبان⟫

How many blessings of your master will you deny?

**------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ BREAK ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------**

---

Symmetry at the sentence level

There is an AYAH in SURAH YASEEN:

> ⟪ar:لَا الشَّمْسُ يَنبَغِي لَهَا أَن تُدْرِكَ الْقَمَرَ وَلَا اللَّيْلُ سَابِقُ النَّهَارِ ۚ وَكُلٌّ فِي فَلَكٍ يَسْبَحُونَ
ک ل ف ی ف ل ک — یسبحون⟫
> *It is not permissible for the sun to reach the moon, nor does the night overtake the day, but each, in an orbit, is rotating.*
> — **Quran 36:40** *(from image; see _provenance.json for validation)*
  (image preserved at ../images/025.png)
  *Note:* Quran 36:40 — celebrated example of Quranic linguistic mimesis: the phrase 'each in an orbit' (kullun fi falakin) is itself a palindrome reading the same forward and backward.

All heavenly bodies are rotating in their orbits. ⟪ar:فَلَكٍۢ⟫means Orbit, and  ⟪ar:يَسْبَحُونَ⟫means "ROTATION".  I want you to keep that in mind, OK? It's really important.

The first thing I want you to notice is that the phrase ⟪ar:كُلٌّۭ فِى فَلَكٍۢ⟫is  a palindrome? It reads the same way forwards and backwards. Now what letter is at the center of this circular composition? It's the letter YA. All other letters are "rotating" around the letter YA. Now check this out! What word did Allah use for rotation? ⟪ar:یسبحون⟫. And what letter does that word begin with? YA! SubhanAllah! The letters are rotating around the very word that Allah uses to say rotation ⟪ar:یسبحون⟫!!! SubhanAllah!!!

How do you do that? How can human beings come up with this kind of symmetry, in spoken text? You see, if I asked you to create a palandrome, the one and only thing you will have to be concerned about is "spelling". And when you take spelling into consideration, you will naturally compromise on the content! But this AYAH, even though a palandrome, it does not compromise on it's content one bit! Allah is not only telling the ancient Arabs about a scientific reality, which is only going to be proved a century later! Not only is he telling us about heavenly bodies, rotating in a circle in a loop, but he says it using words that are in a loop. He tells us using letters that are themselves in rotation; and they are rotating around the very letter, that he uses to say the word rotation! AllahuAkbar!

Is the most intelligent, most eloquent human being in the world capable of doing this in speech? Can the smartest man on earth spontaneously spit out palandromes with such perfection? In a manner that not only does not compromise the content, but actually highlights its significance!  SubhanAllah!!! This content was "spoken" to the Arabs. We are baffled even in the way it is spelled! Absolutely mesmerizing ; absolutely stunning in the perfection of its form.

---

Symmetry between 2 Surahs

So we saw symmetry at the SURAH level, and we saw the same symmetry at the phrase level. Now let's look at symmetry between two SURAHS. I'll call this a combination palendrome. We're going to look at a combination of 2 SURAHS that occur in sequence in the Quran. The 55th SURAH which is Al-REHMAN and the 56th SURAH which is SURAH AL-WAQIAH. We'll go in reverse order; I'm going to talk about SURAH WAQIAH first; then Surah AlRehman... OK?

SURAH WAQIAH has 5 main subjects

[diagram: Five-box outline of Sura al-Waqi'ah (Q56): (1) Sabiqun / the Elite, (2) Companions of the Right, (3) Companions of the Left, (4) Things only Allah can do, (5) Greatness and glory of Quran.]
  (see ../images/026.png)
  *Arabic labels in image:* ⟪ar:سورۃ الواقعۃ · سابقون · أصحاب الیمین · أصحاب الشمال⟫
  *Note:* Topical outline of Sura al-Waqi'ah.

So 5 topics of Surah Al-Waqiah...

The first topic describes a group of people that Allah considers as the Elite

⟪ar-quote:وَٱلسَّبِقُونَ ٱلسَّبِقُونَ أُو۟لَٓئِكَ ٱلْمُقَرَّبُونَ فِى جَنَّتِ ٱلنَّعِيمِ⟫

The first of the foremost. These are the higest ranking people in the jannah, and Allah talks about them right in the beginning of the SURAH. Let's call this topic... "Elite group in heaven"

In the second topic of SURAH AlWAQIAH, Allah mentions another group of people ⟪ar-quote:وَأَصْحَبُ ٱلْيَمِينِ⟫people of the right hand. Where are these people? They are in Jannah too, but in the next level of paradise. A level that is lower than the elite. And then the SURAH gives a description of this level of paradise:

⟪ar-quote:وَأَصْحَبُ ٱلْيَمِينِ مَآ أَصْحَبُ ٱلْيَمِينِ.  فِى سِدْرٍۢ مَّخْضُودٍۢ.  وَطَلْحٍۢ مَّنضُودٍۢ.  وَظِلٍّۢ مَّمْدُودٍۢ . وَمَآءٍۢ مَّسْكُوبٍۢ⟫

Various descriptions of what they will find in Jannah. Now the people of the right hand are also people of Jannah, YES? So Allah first talks about  ⟪ar:ٱلسَّبِقُونَ ٱلسَّبِقُونَ⟫ , meaning the premium package; the highest level, the best people. And then he talks about the rest of the poeple who also made it onboard. In other words, there is the business class JANNAH and then there is the economy class JANNAH as well. So 2 classes of JANNAH are mentioned, but they're both good; people of  both are making it. These are people who have been saved. OK!

The third topic of Surah Waqiah, are people of the left hand... ⟪ar:وَأَصْحَبُ ٱلشِّمَالِ⟫ . Now where are these people located? In JAHANNUM (hell fire); and Allah gives a detailed description of what all is included in the hell package.

⟪ar-quote:وَأَصْحَبُ ٱلشِّمَالِ مَآ أَصْحَبُ ٱلشِّمَالِ.  فِى سَمُومٍۢ وَحَمِيمٍۢ . وَظِلٍّۢ مِّن يَحْمُومٍۢ . لَّا بَارِدٍۢ وَلَا كَرِيمٍ⟫

Allah describes the various torments these people of hellfire will face. These are the people of the left hand who are in danger.

So far we discussed 3 topics; or 3 groups of people. Two groups of people who are saved, ⟪ar:ٱلسَّبِقُونَ ٱلسَّبِقُونَ⟫ the first and the foremost, the ⟪ar:أَصْحَبُ ٱلْيَمِينِ⟫ people of the right hand. And the 3rd group which is ⟪ar:أَصْحَبُ ٱلشِّمَالِ⟫. People of the left hand, who are people of the hell fire. So two good and one bad so far;

Fourth topic: Allah states a list of things that ONLY HE can do. Things that you and I cannot do. And he challenges mankind by asking questions like:

⟪ar-quote:أَفَرَءَيْتُم مَّا تُمْنُونَ?  ءَأَنتُمْ تَخْلُقُونَهُۥ أَمْ نَحْنُ ٱلْخَلِقُون؟⟫

Do you not see the seeds? Did you create the seeds or do we create them?

⟪ar-quote:‏أَفَرَءَيْتُم مَّا تَحْرُثُونَ ؟

‎ ءَأَنتُمْ تَزْرَعُونَهُۥ؟  أَمْ نَحْنُ ٱلزَّرِعُونَ⟫

Do you not see what you sow in the ground? Do you make the plants grow out of the soil, or do we make them grow?

⟪ar-quote:أَفَرَءَيْتُمُ ٱلْمَآءَ ٱلَّذِى تَشْرَبُونَ؟ ءَأَنتُمْ أَنزَلْتُمُوهُ مِنَ ٱلْمُزْنِ أَمْ نَحْنُ ٱلْمُنزِلُونَ⟫؟

Don't you see the water that you drink? Do you bring it down from the skies or do we bring it down?

So the fourth subject, are a list of things that ONLY Allah can do and we cannot do. So let's call this topic, "Things only Allah can do".

We have 4 topics now. What's the first one? "Elite group in heaven". What was the second one? People of right hand. What was the third one? People of left hand. What was the fourth one? Things only Allah can do!

The fifth and final subject of this surah is;

⟪ar-quote:فَلَآ أُقْسِمُ بِمَوَقِعِ ٱلنُّجُومِ.  وَإِنَّهُۥ لَقَسَمٌۭ لَّوْ تَعْلَمُونَ عَظِيمٌ.  إِنَّهُۥ لَقُرْآنٌۭ كَرِيمٌۭ⟫

It is a passage about the greatness and the glory of the Quran. It is about the power of the Quran itself. How the Quran is AWESOME! 

So now we have 5 main subjects of Surah AlWaqiah.

1. The Elite group in heaven

2. People of right hand

3. People of left hand

4. Things only Allah can do

5. The greatness and glory of the Quran

---

What was the surah before Surah AlWaqiah. Surah Rehman. Now guess how many subjects Surah Al-Rehman has?! Yup! 5 subjects!

[diagram: Two-column comparison of Sura al-Rahman (Q55, purple, reading upward 1→5) and Sura al-Waqi'ah (Q56, red, reading downward 1→5), showing how al-Waqi'ah inverts and mirrors al-Rahman's thematic order.]
  (see ../images/027.png)
  *Arabic labels in image:* ⟪ar:سورۃ الواقعۃ · سورۃ الرحمن⟫
  *Note:* Inter-surah chiasm: al-Rahman and al-Waqi'ah read as mirrored sequences — major example in Ismaili Quranic literary analysis.

Subject Number 1:

⟪ar-quote:ٱلرَّحْمَنُ عَلَّمَ ٱلْقُرْآنَ . خَلَقَ ٱلْإِنسَنَ . عَلَّمَهُ ٱلْبَيَانَ⟫

The greatness of the Quran, for his greatest creation - Al-Insaan. Taught by the intensely merciful AlRehman himself. What was the last subject of Surah AlWaqiah? "Greatness and glory of Quran"

Subject Number 2 in Surah Al-Rehman,

⟪ar-quote:ٱلشَّمْسُ وَٱلْقَمَرُ بِحُسْبَانٍۢ . وَٱلنَّجْمُ وَٱلشَّجَرُ يَسْجُدَانِ . وَٱلسَّمَآءَ رَفَعَهَا وَوَضَعَ ٱلْمِيزَانَ⟫

Oh my goodness. Subject number 2 of Surah Rehman; the creations of Allah that only Allah can create: the sun, the moon, the stars. What was the second last subject of Surah AlWaqiah? Things only Allah can do!

The first subject of Surah Rehman is the greatness of the Quran, the last subject of Surah AlWaqiah is greatness of the quran.

The second subject of Surah Rehman is Things only Allah can create, the second last subject of Surah AlWaqiah are things only Allah can do

Subject Number 3 of Surah Rehman. It is about judment day and about criminals that will end up in the hell fire...

⟪ar-quote:سَنَفْرُغُ لَكُمْ أَيُّهَ ٱلثَّقَلَانِ.  يُرْسَلُ عَلَيْكُمَا شُوَاظٌۭ مِّن نَّارٍۢ.  وَنُحَاسٌۭ فَلَا تَنتَصِرَانِ . فَإِذَا ٱنشَقَّتِ ٱلسَّمَآءُ فَكَانَتْ وَرْدَةًۭ كَٱلدِّهَانِ .

فَيَوْمَئِذٍۢ لَّا يُسْـَٔلُ عَن ذَنۢبِهِ إِنسٌۭ وَلَا جَآنٌّۭ.  يُعْرَفُ ٱلْمُجْرِمُونَ بِسِيمَهُمْ فَيُؤْخَذُ بِٱلنَّوَصِى وَٱلْأَقْدَامِ.

  هَذِهِۦ جَهَنَّمُ ٱلَّتِى يُكَذِّبُ بِهَا ٱلْمُجْرِمُونَ.  يَطُوفُونَ بَيْنَهَا وَبَيْنَ حَمِيمٍ آنٍۢ⟫

Detailed description of the people of hell fire...

What was the third last subject in Surah AlWaqiah? People of the left hand. People of the hell.

Subject Number 4 ...

⟪ar-quote:وَلِمَنْ خَافَ مَقَامَ رَبِّهِۦ جَنَّتَانِ⟫

There are 2 jannah for people who fear Allah; and then he describes those 2 jannah. He explains what all is included in this package...

⟪ar-quote:ذَوَاتَآ أَفْنَانٍۢ . فِيهِمَا عَيْنَانِ تَجْرِيَانِ.  فِيهِمَا مِن كُلِّ فَكِهَةٍۢ زَوْجَانِ . مُتَّكِـِٔينَ عَلَىٰ فُرُشٍۭ بَطَآئِنُهَا مِنْ إِسْتَبْرَقٍۢ .

وَجَنَى ٱلْجَنَّتَيْنِ دَانٍۢ.  فِيهِنَّ قَصِرَتُ ٱلطَّرْفِ لَمْ يَطْمِثْهُنَّ إِنسٌۭ قَبْلَهُمْ وَلَا جَآنٌّۭ . كَأَنَّهُنَّ ٱلْيَاقُوتُ وَٱلْمَرْجَانُ . هَلْ جَزَآءُ ٱلْإِحْسَنِ إِلَّا ٱلْإِحْسَنُ⟫

He describes these jannah at length. And then immediatel after that:

Subject Number 5...

⟪ar-quote:وَمِن دُونِهِمَا جَنَّتَانِ⟫

And in addition to that, and above and beyond that, I have two more awesome jannah for you. The special package! What's included in this special package?

⟪ar-quote:مُدْهَآمَّتَانِ . فِيهِمَا عَيْنَانِ نَضَّاخَتَانِ . فِيهِمَا فَكِهَةٌۭ وَنَخْلٌۭ وَرُمَّانٌۭ . فِيهِنَّ خَيْرَتٌ حِسَانٌۭ.  حُورٌۭ مَّقْصُورَتٌۭ فِى ٱلْخِيَامِ.

  لَمْ يَطْمِثْهُنَّ إِنسٌۭ قَبْلَهُمْ وَلَا جَآنٌّۭ . مُتَّكِـِٔينَ عَلَىٰ رَفْرَفٍ خُضْرٍۢ وَعَبْقَرِىٍّ حِسَانٍۢ⟫

BEAUTIFUL BEAUTIFUL AYAATS. InshaAllah I'd love to study Surah Rehman in detail with you in one of the future sessions

But anyway, he talks about JANNAH 2 times. The economy package first and the delux package last. Subjects four and five of SURAH REHMAN. What were the second and first subjets of Surah Waqiah? In reverse order

⟪ar-quote:اصحاب الیمن⟫and ⟪ar-quote:السابقون السابقون⟫.

Subject number 1 and subject number 5, both about the higher level of jannah.

Subject number 2 and subject number 4, both about a lower level of jannah... Subhan Allah! He talks about the higest janna first in Surah Waqiah, he talks about the highest janna last in Surah Rehman. He talks about the lower janna second in Surah Waqiah, he talks about the lower janna second to last in Surah Rehman.

Things only Allah can do is mentioned 2nd in SURAH REHMAN and second to last in SURAH WAQIAH.

Greatness and Glory of Quran last in SURAH WAQIAH, and first in SURAH REHMAN

SubhanAllah! Perfect Perfect symmetry! How do you do that with spoken text? Two completely different surahs, coming together in perfect symmetry... AllahuAkbar!

Symmetrical in a single AYAH

Now my personal favorite. Ayat Al-Kursi. This one single AYAH is made up of 9 sentences, OK? 9 independent sentences coming together to form one single AYAH

[diagram: Color-blocked teaching tile of Ayatul Kursi (Quran 2:255) with each clause's translation tagged by color and English summary. Low resolution but recognizable as the standard Throne Verse decomposition.]
  (see ../images/028.png)
  *Arabic labels in image:* ⟪ar:آیۃ الکرسی⟫
  *Note:* Ayatul Kursi (Quran 2:255) — full verse decomposition into ~8 clauses.

Now of course you've already guessed, that this too is a plaindrome. So I'll just make this simpler and we'll go over the translation of each one of these sentences, symmetrically. We'll compare the first and the last; then the second and the second last, the third and the third from last and so on. So let's begin with the first and the last sentence.

The first one...

⟪ar-quote:ٱللَّهُ لَآ إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ ٱلْحَىُّ ٱلْقَيُّومُ⟫

This beautiful sentence ends with 2 of Allah's names. What are those 2 names? ⟪ar:الحی⟫The everliving, and ⟪ar:القیوم⟫The source of all establishment; or the source of all maintenance - The ever watchful! ⟪ar:قیوم⟫has many meanings. It basically means that everything stands and exists, and is maintained because of Allah. So not only does he create, he also keeps any eye on it! If he only created, and didn't maintain, creations would get destroyed. He is the ultimate creator and He is the ultimate maintainer. And by virtue and combination of these qualities of ⟪ar:الحی القیوم⟫ , what does that make Him? To answer that, join this sentence to the 9th sentence.

⟪ar-quote:وَهُوَ ٱلْعَلِىُّ ٱلْعَظِيمُ⟫

And He is the lofty and the mighty. Lofty by virtue of being the creator; and Mighty by virtue of maintaining them. Two attributes of Allah mentioned in the first sentence: الحی القیوم; two attributes mentioned in the last sentence: العلی العظیم. Perfect Symmetry!

---

Now let's look at the second and 8th sentence
⟪ar-quote:لَا تَأْخُذُهُۥ سِنَةٌۭ وَلَا نَوْمٌۭ⟫

Drowsiness and sleep do not even touch him.

You kids know what drowsiness means, right? You know that strange feeling you have during lectures in your classroom - that's drowsiness ! Where your eyes start closing a little bit. You're not actually sleeping but you're just about ready to go into dreamland. That is what's called  "Sinah" in Arabic. And the next step right after that is "Naum" which means deep sleep. First comes Sinah, then comes Naum. These are both things that creations have. When living creatures get tired, they start feeling drowsy and then eventually they fall into deep sleep.

Before we talk about its pair sentence, I want to tell you something about security. Security guards have the hardest job in the world. Why?  Because it's the most boring job on the planet. What do you always find the security guard doing in movies? Either staring at the CC TV monitors - and it's the same damn picture for 12 hours straight. They're staring at the white, scratched and beat up toyota parked in the same spot for hours. It's not a proshe or a lamburgini; not even a Mercedeze Benz. OR, they're sitting on a chair staring into space for hours and hours. Not the most exciting job you can have in life. Especially if you're a college student. So what tends to happen when you're guarding something? You tend to get sleepy; you tend to get tired. That's why, eventually what you always find every security guard doing is what? Sleeping!

But Allah says in the 8the sentence...

⟪ar-quote:وَلَا يَـُٔودُهُۥ حِفْظُهُمَا⟫

Guarding the skies and the earth, does not exhaust Allah. What does guarding something bring for us human beings? Drowsiness and Sleep! Sinah and Naum! But Allah says not me! I guard all my creation, but I never get exhausted. I never feel drowsy and I never sleep on the job. Perfect symmetry!!

---

What's the third ayah?

⟪ar-quote:⟪ar-quote:لَّهُۥ مَا فِى ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَمَا فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ⟫⟫

He owns whatever is in the heavens and whatever is in the earth. Before I can explain this connection to you, I need you to understand the difference between 2 arabic words: ⟪ar:مالک⟫and ⟪ar:مَلِک⟫... Because it'll make you appreciate these ayats like nothing else. ⟪ar:مالک⟫means an owner; ⟪ar:مَلِک⟫means a king. Is there a difference between a king and an owner? Yes! You are the owner of your pen. But you never say, I am the royal sovereign king of this pen! right? That wouldn't t make a lot of sense. You understand? People can be owners of small things. You can own a car, you can own a pen, you can own a phone, a computer; but you cannot own a kingdom. Only a  king would have a kingdom.

Here's another difference. Ownership is always about property. But kingdom is not specifically about property. You're never a king over a tree, or the king over a piece of land. You are a king over all the people that live in that land. Kingdom is about controlling people; while ownership is about controlling objects. There's a big difference. Ownership is at the micro level, whereas kingdom is at the macro level.
Allah says..  ⟪ar-quote:⟪ar-quote:لَّهُۥ مَا فِى ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَمَا فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ⟫⟫

I have the ownership of everything thats in the heavens; and everything thats in the earth. What is the AYAH about? Ownership or kingdom? It's about ownership! Because Allah says every-"thing" in the heavens and earth belongs to me. In other words, every single thing in creation is owned by Allah.

Now let's look at the third last sentence?

⟪ar-quote:⟪ar-quote:وَسِعَ كُرْسِيُّهُ ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضَ⟫⟫

His throne extends to the skies and the earths. Allah talks about his throne. Who has a throne? A king has a throne. So when he's talking about his throne, is he talking about ownership or kingdom?  He's talking about his kingdom!  So you see, while the previous sentence was about ownership; this sentence is about kingdom! And they both come together completing the picture! Because if you're just an owner, you're not a king. If you're just a king, you're not necessarily an owner. You can be the king of an island, but does that mean you own every house on that island. No! You might own your house, but are you the king of the house? No! But Allah is not only the owner of all things... He is also the king of all things... ! He is ⟪ar:مالک⟫and he is also ⟪ar:مَلِک⟫.

The attribute of Allah being an owner (مالک ) is declared in ⟪ar:لَّهُۥ مَا فِى ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَمَا فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ⟫ and Allah being the king is declared in ⟪ar:وَسِعَ كُرْسِيُّهُ ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضَ.⟫

---

⟪ar-quote:⟪ar-quote:مَن ذَا ٱلَّذِى يَشْفَعُ عِندَهُۥ إِلَّا بِإِذْنِهِ⟫⟫

Who will come and make ⟪ar:شفاعۃ⟫with Allah unless he gives permission. Let's first understand the word ⟪ar:شفاعۃ.⟫ If you look at the translation in the image, it has a big English words Intercession! Let's make it simple. ⟪ar:شفاعۃ⟫basically means, you've got connections! You've got people! So if I am about to lose my job, but my uncle is the manager of the company and he comes and says... No No No... He's with me! He's good! That's ⟪ar:شفاعۃ⟫. Your dad is the chief of staff of a hospital, especially if you're in Pakistan or India, and so you get to go in the Emergency unit even if you have a headache. You get called in first! That's ⟪ar:شفاعۃ⟫. The guy with the fractured skull can wait!

So Allah says, on the day of judgment who would dares make ⟪ar:شفاعۃ⟫ . Who would dare Intercede except without *my* permission! In other words, ONLY the people he selects, can make ⟪ar:شفاعۃ⟫; not everyone. You understand? Allah is about to throw someone in hell, I can't just step forward and say, woa woa woa Allah mian! He's with me! :))))) No... He'll throw me along with him. So nobody will have the right to make ⟪ar:شفاعۃ⟫on behalf of anyone else except the one he chooses. And the one He has chosen is his beloved messenger Muhammad Mustafa (SA). We beg Allah to let us all qualify for his intercession on that day. Because he clearly says that nobody else will come for you on judgment day. It's not going to happen.

So this sentence is about nobody having any authority unless Allah gives that authority to them. The only exception is by Allah's permission. IF Allah gives permission, someone can interceed otherwise nobody can say anything on that day. Everyone clear about that?

Now let's look at its pair...

⟪ar-quote:⟪ar-quote:وَلَا يُحِيطُونَ بِشَىْءٍۢ مِّنْ عِلْمِهِۦٓ إِلَّا بِمَا شَآءَ⟫⟫

They know nothing, they have no power, they encompass nothing of his knowledge ⟪ar:إِلَّا⟫, except; ⟪ar:بِمَا شَآءَ⟫of what HE wills. Both statements are about the exceptions that ONLY Allah has. In the first sentence, nobody can intercede EXCEPT the one who has the permission of Allah. In the connecting sentence, nobody can gain anything from his knowledge EXCEPT the one who He chooses. SubhanAllah!

---

Now what's left? The center statement..

⟪ar-quote:⟪ar-quote:يَعْلَمُ مَا بَيْنَ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَمَا خَلْفَهُم⟫⟫

OMG! He says He knows what is ahead of them and what is behind them. He knows that everything that is coming before this statement is in perfect correlation, perfect symmetry with what's coming ahead of this statement.... AllahuAkbar!! Right in the middle he is saying, I know what's before and I know what's coming after. He literally makes this statement the center of the circle. The radius of one end, will be equal to the radius of the other end. SubhanAllah! Who can speak like that?? 

Again, remember, we read the Quran as a book. But did Rasul Allah recite like that? Did he say that look sentence number 1 and 9 and 2 and 8 and 3 and 7, and 4 and 6 are in perfect correlation to the 5th sentence? No! This is spoken word! He was just speaking the Quran. We are able to see these things today when they were put in writing. But look how marvellous the Quran is. In its speech as well as in its written form. When is there a greater chance of mistake? When you write something or when you say something? When you say something! Once you say it, it is very hard to take it back. Especially if it's on youtube!  AllahuAkbar! For example, if you're writing a nasty email to your cousin; before you hit send, you can think about it and tone it down. You can rephrase things, and finaly just say Ashoora Mubarak and send it. You have a chance to take it back.. But you can't do that in spoken word. When you say something, as soon as you've said it, you're done! No room to edit; no room to fix it. And Allah did not reveal this quran in writing; he revealed it in speech!

---

Symmetry in two consecutive AYATS

In Surah REHMAN and Surah WAQIAH, we saw 2 consequiteve Surahs coming together to form a perfect palandrome. Now let's look at 2 consequtive AYAATS that come together to form a palindrome.

Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) says in Surah Al-Jumuah. These are the first 2 ayats

⟪ar-quote:يُسَبِّحُ لِلَّهِ مَا فِى ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَمَا فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ ٱلْمَلِكِ ٱلْقُدُّوسِ ٱلْعَزِيزِ ٱلْحَكِيمِ⟫

⟪ar-quote:هُوَ ٱلَّذِى بَعَثَ فِى ٱلْأُمِّيِّۦنَ رَسُولًۭا مِّنْهُمْ يَتْلُوا۟ عَلَيْهِمْ آيَتِهِۦ وَيُزَكِّيهِمْ وَيُعَلِّمُهُمُ ٱلْكِتَبَ وَٱلْحِكْمَةَ وَإِن كَانُوا۟ مِن قَبْلُ لَفِى ضَلَلٍۢ مُّبِينٍۢ⟫

Those of you who read the Quran regularly must have noticed that in most AYATS Allah ends the AYAH by referring to 2 of his names

⟪ar-quote:غفور الرحیم ؛ عزیزٌ حکیم ؛ عزیزٌ انْتقام⟫

You'll see that Allah mentiones 2 of his names many many times in the Quran. Always a name pair is used. But if you notice in the first ayah of Surah Jumuah, there is something unique:

⟪ar-quote:يُسَبِّحُ لِلَّهِ مَا فِى ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَمَا فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ ٱلْمَلِكِ ٱلْقُدُّوسِ ٱلْعَزِيزِ ٱلْحَكِيمِ⟫

Allah uses 4 names at the end of this ayah.

The first is Malik, which I just explained, means king.

The second is Al-Quddoos; which means the perfectly pure. Or we can translate it as the source of all purity

Then Al-Azeez, which means the one with ultimate authority

Finally there is AlHakeem, which means the wise.

Repeat

Now who is the first AYAH talking about?

⟪ar-quote:يُسَبِّحُ لِلَّهِ مَا فِى ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَمَا فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ ٱلْمَلِكِ ٱلْقُدُّوسِ ٱلْعَزِيزِ ٱلْحَكِيمِ⟫

Everything in the heavens and the earth glorify Allah. He is the King, the Pure, The Authority, the Wise. The first AYAH is talking about Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) !

Who is the second AYAH talking about?

⟪ar-quote:هُوَ ٱلَّذِى بَعَثَ فِى ٱلْأُمِّيِّۦنَ رَسُولًۭا مِّنْهُمْ يَتْلُوا۟ عَلَيْهِمْ آيَتِهِۦ وَيُزَكِّيهِمْ وَيُعَلِّمُهُمُ ٱلْكِتَبَ وَٱلْحِكْمَةَ⟫

It is He who has sent for the people of Mecca, a Messenger from among themselves; reciting to them his verses and purifying them and teaching them the Book and wisdom -

Who is this ayat talking about? Rasul Allah

This is also one of the most beautiful AYATS of the Quran, because in this one verse, Allah has summarized the entire SEERAH of the prophet (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). The entire SEERAH in one single AYAH. Because in this AYAH Allah talks about the 4 steps his beloved messenger Rasul Allah (SA) took in order to transform society. How many steps did he take? 4 steps!  What were those 4 steps?
⟪ar-quote:يَتْلُوا۟ عَلَيْهِمْ آيَتِهِ

وَيُزَكِّيهِمْ

وَيُعَلِّمُهُمُ ٱلْكِتَبَ

وَٱلْحِكْمَةَ⟫

Hmmm... Where did we hear the number 4 before?? How many names of Allah were mentioned? And His messenger follows how many steps? Now let's take a step back and let me give you something to think about.

Imagine you live in a time let's say 4000 of years ago. You just bought your brand new donkey and you're taking it out for a spin. And now as you're travelling, you see that you are entering into a brand new kingdom. How would you know you're entering a new kingdom? Through signs of the kingdom! Flags? Statues! Monuments! right? You notice soldiers that bear the mark of the king. You might notice a castle. In other words, you will see certain signs that will tell you that this is a kingdom, or that this place has a king! Because a king is known by his signs and symbols. You will not know someone is king unless you see him wearing a crown. He has to have sign and symbols: a crown, a castle, a throne; these are all signs that you are dealing with a king! So my first point, is that a king is known by his signs.

What was the first name of Allah mentioned? AlMalik! What does it mean? King! In the very next Allah says that his messenger does 4 things. What is the first one? The first one is

⟪ar-quote:يَتْلُوا۟ عَلَيْهِمْ آيَتِهِ⟫

He reads on to the people the king's signs! How is a king known again? By his signs! And the messenger tells the people Allah's signs! He makes them notice Allah's kingdom? You see those mountains over there? It's part of his kingdom! You see that sun over there? it's part of his kingdom! You seen that moon in the night? it's part of his kingdom! That's how you know you're dealing with a king. You see the stars at night? That's the kingdom of Allah. He is known by his signs.

---

What was the second name of Allah in the first ayah? AlQudoos! What did it mean? Source of all purity. Now what's the second thing the messenger does?

⟪ar-quote:وَيُزَكِّيهِمْ⟫

He purifies them! He reads the kings signs to them, and he does what? He Purifies them. You see a connection?

---

What was the third name of Allah that was mentioned? AlAzeez! What did it mean? Ultimate authority!

Where do laws come from? Laws come from an authority! In a house, rules come from the parents; it does not come from the child. Because parents have what? Authority! In a class room the rules come from the teacher; rules don't come from the students, because the teacher has authority! In a country, the rules come from the government! It comes from the poeple making the laws;  it comes from the courts, not the common people. Allah says..

⟪ar-quote:وَيُعَلِّمُهُمُ ٱلْكِتَبَ⟫

He teaches them the book! And the word book in Arabic literature is used for "law". So it's like saying that he teaches them the law! And law can only be given by the proper authority. In other words, AlAzeez is the only one who can make alKitaab. You cannot make kitaab without having ⟪ar:عزۃ⟫. You cannot have law without an authority. And BTW even in English literature we say, the judge threw the book at him! That does not mean that the judge got angry and opend his skull by thrwoing a 15 lb book at the plaintiff. No! It means that the judge used the full extent of the law against that person. Or if someone says I'm going to do this by the book. What does that mean? I'm going to do this according to the law! That's by the book. So AlAzeez is the authority and the messenger teaches the law dictated by the authority. Therefore⟪ar:وَيُعَلِّمُهُمُ ٱلْكِتَبَ⟫

---

What was the last name of Allah mentioned in this sequence? AlHakeem! The Wise! Allahs says

⟪ar-quote:وَيُعَلِّمُهُمُ ٱلْكِتَبَ وَٱلْحِكْمَةَ⟫

He teaches them wisdom! Where does wisdome come from? It comes from the wise! 4 names of Allah in the first AYAH; 4 activities of the messenger in the next AYAH and they're each corelated perfectly. It took me 20 minutes to explain this to you; but Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) just says it. He just says it! What human being is able to think this way. Hmmmm... I just said 4 names of Allah, I should now back them up with 4 steps, 4 verbs that correlate with the previous names in the same order. Who can do that? It's beyond human capability; and RasulAllah just creates these miracles spontaneously! SubhanAllah! We just read through these miracles without appreciating them. We just pass through these powerful observations without realizing what we just read; and WALLAHEE when we do realize them, we are left mesmerized. We are incapacitated! We are left incapable of a response. AllahuAkbar!

Conclusion

AlHamdulillah! That brings us to the end of our journey of exploring of miracles. If you remember, we began these sessions by asking a simple question. We first established the fact, based on historical evidence, that the message of Quran was delivered as an unscripted, impromptu speech before a live audience, comprising of family, friends and enemies. We established that it was impossible for this message to be pre-meditated simply based on the conditions under which it was revealed. The Quran was being revealed as the messenger was going through a slew of emotions. And we all know how our conversations are affected by hightened emotions. But the thing about the Quran was that once it was revealed, once the messenger uttered these words of revelation, there was no going back. So we established that the Quran could not have been a scripted or a premeditated speech. The only question that was left to answer was: Is the Quran human speech? or is it divine speech? Is Quran a product of human effort? or is it a product of divine revelation? Is it ⟪ar:معجزۃ⟫or not?

And so I defined the word miracle ⟪ar:اعجاز⟫for you; and explained that ⟪ar:اعجاز⟫comes from the word ⟪ar:عجز⟫which means to completely defeat someone. To bring someone down to their knees; to incapacitate somone; to render one incapable of a response.

And then I told you that the most amazing aspect of this Quran, is that it is a "living" miracle. If you remember when I said, that when an athiest comes and asks us if the Quran is a miracle, our response is so different from the kind of response a Christian or a Jew would give about their books. They are forced to believe the divinity of their books on blind faith. We on the other hand, hold this living miracle in our hands; and we can re-create its miracles for us as well as others as many times as we want.

And so basing all these sessions on the definition of the word "miracle", I showed you that the Quran is miraculous, not in one single dimension, but in so many different dimensions. It is miraculous in it's speech; it is miraculous in its choice of words; it is miraculous in its order of words; it is miraculous in its eloquence; it is miraculous in its conciseness; it is miraculous in its effect on a gloabal and societal level, as well as on an individual and personal level; it is miraculous in its scientific dimensions; it is miraculous in its form of preservation - that even today, 1400 years later, not a single attack can hold up against the Quran. Even in its book form, it is miraculous in its unique structure; It is miraculous in its balance of words.  And if all of these dimensions weren't enough, the Quran is also incredible miraculous in its compiled form; in its symmetrical structure.

And everything that I have shared with you, is not even the tip of the iceberg. Everything I've showed you so far is simply the external shine of the Quran. You know, how when you walk into a showroom to purchase a brand new car, the first thing that attracts you is the shape of the car and its color? That's all we've seen of the Quran so far. We have only looked at its outward shine. We have not even peeked inside it yet. We have not yet experienced the luxury of this car. We have not yet taken it out for a test-drive. Everything you've seen so far is simply the outer - surface level stuff of the Quran. And if you agree with me, that the exterior is truly miraculous, then WALLAHEE, its interior is exponentially miraculous. If the external beauty of the Quran has captured your heart, mesmerized you - wait till you see its inner beauty - which is the actual widsoms and the teachings of this Quran.

So now at this point only two things are possible. Either you are aboslutely convinced that this is indeed divine speech; or you're still in doubt about this Quran being the message of God. If you're still "not" convinced, then let me tell you, in my personal opinion, there is nothing else in this world that can, or will convince you. Because this is the very proof that Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) gave his messenger to "prove" to mankind that He exists. So if everything I shared with you is not good enough, nothing will be!

But if you are now convinced, that this is in fact a divine message, then that conviction comes with certain responsibilities. You've heard the famous expression: "With knowledge comes responsibility"? So if this is the message of Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala), then everything that is said in this book must also be true. That has to be our attitudes moving forward. Now could there still be things in this book that might not make sense when we read them? Sure! But now, where's the problem? Is Allah the problem? Is there is a problem with this message? Or is there a problem withou our understanding? It must be with "our" understanding of this message. Because we've already now experienced that this book and its message are flawless. Which means that we are the ones that need to put in the effort to understand this book. If this paradigm shift, this surrender, does not take place, then there was really no point in experiencing all of these miracles.

Because we've already put Allah on trial, to determine if this is his message or not. In last 10 sessions, we were the judge and Quran was the plaintiff. In every session we put the Quran in the stands and asked it, "Are you the message of God?". And in all 10 sessions, it proved to all of us, without the shadow of a doubt, that indeed it is a divine message. And so now that the Quran has been acquited of all blame, of being the product of a human effort, the next step is to turn that initial perception on its head To now see ourselves as being on trial! We are now the ones on trial; we are now the ones in the stand; and Quran is now our judge. This now becomes the primarly goal of the study of Quran. How do I understand the wisdom of this message, and how do I align my life in accordance with it.
